<Review>I visited during Covid so naturally the arrangements and decorations were not like you would see in pre-covid pictures. However, I was pleasantly surprised with how peaceful, calm and well maintained the temple was. That's exactly how a place of worship should be in order to invoke positive vibrations from within.

I visited at around 6 pm on Saturday evening when only a couple of people were around. Ample parking space was available. I did not see any stand to remove shoes. The interior is fully carpeted.</Review>< Pics>

First Timer! I tried orange theory fitness today for my first class and it was a lot of fun! I read about it online before I went so I kind of had an idea of how their system works but once you get there they go into way more detail. Casey was my trainer today and he showed me how to use their treadmills and row machines before class began. The 60 minute class went by pretty fast and your always moving except for 30 seconds rest in between certain workouts. The workouts are challenging at least for myself who hasn't worked out consistently in a long time. Casey was a great trainer, motivating and checking in with everyone working out throughout the class. At first I felt a little intimated by the different machines and getting the hang of things but picked up on it pretty fast. I enjoyed the different workouts that we did today and the fast pace of things to keep your heart rate up and burning calories. I purchased 4 classes in a month package just to start but I can see myself going more often if my schedule allows. If your interested in trying it out I say go for it! I burned 600 calories in 1 hour and that's way more than I would burn working out myself at my other gym.</Review>

<user_id>117417319259273041235<//user_id><Name>Gregory Tada<//Name><Date>1543113086572</Date><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
To some of the previous reviewers: FFS it's not ramen, okay? Don't expect tonkotsu broth. It's UDON.

I just ate here with the family and enjoyed it. There aren't many udon shops around here, and I was pleasantly surprised to find this in the mall. The broth was flavorful without being overpowering, and the noodles had nice body to them. I had the tempura udon, and while the shrimp was good the potato was a bit hard. Overall it's solid.

I'd usually give this place four stars, but I felt it necessary to offset the lame reviewers expecting ramen.</Review>

<review>This place is located between the promenade and the mall in a very attractive strip of tempting food vendors. This little strip give you the feel of walking through Asia and making you easily drooling for food. It turns out that the place looks better than it taste.
One of the worst ramen I ever had. I am sorry but the instant ramen taste better than this. For 11 dollars I was expecting some bone broth flavors in my tonkatsu ramen. Instead I got a bowl of creamy broth of salty soup that is covered in a layer of unknown orange grease. It was totally off from the image they showed on the menu. They also don't serve their ramen with delicious soft center ramen eggs instead u get soild hard boil egg. The service was slow and they ran out of green onions for the day. I was there at dinner time which is 7pm and you have no more green onions???
Give it one star for the chashu and the seaweed which was the only decent part of my meal.
In conclusion expensive with no satisfaction.< /review>< Pics>

< review>
Tsurumaru is located in the Eat area of the Santa Anita mall, next to Uncle Tetsu Cheesecake. The cashier mentioned that the shrimp tempura udon was a popular favorite, which also happens to be one of the most expensive items in the menu. I did end up ordering the tempura udon.

Upon receiving my entree, the tempura was over fried and dripping with oil. I peeled off the batter and just ate the shrimp and sweet potato. The udon was just ok, nothing special, but wasn't too horrible. However, the broth was super salty. I couldn't get rid of that saltiness after taste for the rest of the day.

Self serve type place where you get your own utensils and bus your own trays. Needless to say, I won't be returning.<//review>
